<h3>Vyvy-vi <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/558192816308617227/af64b80c32205d256106f8da7e88a3ce.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_09-Jun-21 04:10 PM_:

Btw, while looking at the praise lists, I saw a small inconsistency(and the whitespace before octopus' name bothered me... a *bit*) with regard to some of the discord usernames having the user tag(discriminator, the #number), and that made me look at the praise data quantification sheet. In many cases, the sheet just uses usernames, which is unsafe since they are not unique, can change, and are harder to maintain. Even the use of username#number is not fully safe. In most cases, username#discriminator **tends** to be unique ~~unless people have nitro and coincidentally change their discriminator number to match the username and discriminator of another person. (potential chances of impersonation in the DAO. And since the Praise bot doesn't really check IDs, they can potentially just hijack praise, and maybe even get the wallet changed... *though that change is not likely since that needs CS Trusted Seed contact and conversation*)~~ ~~maybe, we should use discord user IDs (these are numeric and unique, or atleast check them in the praise bot, when dishing praise)~~ ~~(this naming issue can also lead to instances where you ping the wrong user, and praise gets sent to different people).~~ ~~Example:~~ ~~My discord usertag-> Vyvy-vi#5040~~ ~~(unsafe, and not "certifiably" unique)~~ ~~My discord user ID-> 558192816308617227~~ ~~(unique, and doesn't change even after name changes)~~ **EDIT: I was wrong, discord does enforce unique id-ing.** (edited)

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/558192816308617227/af64b80c32205d256106f8da7e88a3ce.png](https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/558192816308617227/af64b80c32205d256106f8da7e88a3ce.png)

Vyvy-vi

[Btw, while looking at the praise lists, I saw a small inconsistency(and the whitespace before octopus' name bothered me... a *bit*) with regard to some of the discord usernames having the user tag(discriminator, the #number), and that made me look at the praise data quantification sheet. In many cases, the sheet just uses usernames, which is unsafe since they are not unique, can change, and are harder to maintain. Even the use of username#number is not fully safe. In most cases, username#discriminator **tends** to be unique ~~unless people have nitro and coincidentally change their discriminator number to match the username and discriminator of another person. (potential chances of impersonation in the DAO. And since the Praise bot doesn't really check IDs, they can potentially just hijack praise, and maybe even get the wallet changed... *though that change is not likely since that needs CS Trusted Seed contact and conversation*)~~ ~~maybe, we should use discord user IDs (these are numeric and unique, or atleast check them in the praise bot, when dishing praise)~~ ~~(this naming issue can also lead to instances where you ping the wrong user, and praise gets sent to different people).~~ ~~Example:~~ ~~My discord usertag-> Vyvy-vi#5040~~ ~~(unsafe, and not "certifiably" unique)~~ ~~My discord user ID-> 558192816308617227~~ ~~(unique, and doesn't change even after name changes)~~ **EDIT: I was wrong, discord does enforce unique id-ing.**  (edited)](about:blank#)

[Btw, while looking at the praise lists, I saw a small inconsistency(and the whitespace before octopus' name bothered me... a *bit*) with regard to some of the discord usernames having the user tag(discriminator, the #number), and that made me look at the praise data quantification sheet. In many cases, the sheet just uses usernames, which is unsafe since they are not unique, can change, and are harder to maintain. Even the use of username#number is not fully safe. In most cases, username#discriminator **tends** to be unique ~~unless people have nitro and coincidentally change their discriminator number to match the username and discriminator of another person. _04-Aug-21 02:04 AM_:

Money Talk ‚Äî The group pondered the recent interest of venture capital in the TEC, their desire for providing impact funding and how they fit within our current funding structure

was there any conclusion? The problem with TEC is that most of the urgently needed stuff needs to fund R&D and perhaps education TEacademy ... VCs are notorious in not paying for research (they want markets) and education is inherently a service industry (scalable with humans). So a potential gulf between

***expectations (of x100 returns) vs return to community***

(zero profit). Any input? (edited)

<h3>akrtws (TE Academy) <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/686955086941126683/7aaeae2f15035eb415bb51aaf9ad0878.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_04-Aug-21 04:02 AM_:

Agree @drllau - the freerider problem is a nut to crack - everyone wants to benefit from knowledge created, no-one wants to invest in developing it. But open-source is a great example that we'll be able to find solutions, if we invest into finding smart incentive alignment. First step: actively managing proposals and funds inflow. There should be a dedicated working group, like here: [https://gov.gitcoin.co/t/public-goods-funding-workstream-budget-request/7993](https://gov.gitcoin.co/t/public-goods-funding-workstream-budget-request/7993) It includes managing the treasury, building relationsships to funding partners, managing the proposal process etc.

Public Goods Funding- Workstream Budget Request

Hey Everyone, Below is some motivation for this proposal: There was general sentiment in the seasons proposal that we need ways to reward work done for the DAO more than just stewardship as first order of business Workstreams are good in theory for rewarding contributors, but don‚Äôt yet have teeth in the way Simona proposed in her governance pr...

_04-Aug-21 06:05 AM_:

well TEC (the R&D side) could get investment, but it'll have to be in the form of a loan payable from licensing ... so a bare bones gratis version for academia, a paid plan for startups and the full bells & whistles for enterprises. It'll be hateful but once you take money from a VC, you are on a path to deadline hell (which kills creativity) [https://www.newyorker.com/magazine/2020/01/27/is-venture-capital-worth-the-risk](https://www.newyorker.com/magazine/2020/01/27/is-venture-capital-worth-the-risk) ... see MakerDAO for classic example (edited)

Is Venture Capital Worth the Risk?

The industry shaped the past decade. It could destroy the next.

![https://media.newyorker.com/photos/5e20c8efc7502500083139cf/16:9/w_1280,c_limit/200127_r35389.jpg](https://media.newyorker.com/photos/5e20c8efc7502500083139cf/16:9/w_1280,c_limit/200127_r35389.jpg)

<h3>mitch (üçî, üçî) <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/288019500132073472/f2a7e7eb583ccb9397f85406a3962ec3.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_04-Aug-21 09:08 AM_:

I think this is a larger problem with most token economies.. especially those trying to do it without LM programs .. @akrtws (TE Academy) Do you know any great projects that have made robust use cases for their tokens?

<h3>akrtws (TE Academy) <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/686955086941126683/7aaeae2f15035eb415bb51aaf9ad0878.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_04-Aug-21 10:04 AM_:

Wait, don't mix cause and effect here. The reason why we have tokens without "robust use cases" is not that there aren't any, it's rather that financing projects via an *initial* token launch has become feasible. And developing use cases is the key objective to put the funds collected to work. Additionally, 8 of the top 12 tokens in DeFi are governance tokens, and token buyers bet on the future value of governance as a capital. Considering TEC as a governance token, you could discuss the value of the underlying ecosystem to be governed - what makes our ecosystem valuable? And why is it relevant to hold a token and have a say in distributing the funds? Again, I don't want to imply that we won't find great answers, I just think we should address these questions actively.

Elinor Ostrom Day - Institut Ostrom Catalunya

Online Summit Day: September 23rd Time: 10:00 (NYC) / 15:00 (London) / 16:00 (Barcelona) In 2009, Elinor Ostrom won the Nobel Prize in Economic Sciences for her contributions to the governance of shared resources. Ostrom‚Äôs work showed the value of building multinational, multidisciplinary, and comparative research bridging the social and natural...

_29-Sep-21 01:07 PM_:

**The first official vote of the Hatch DAO has started. The vote ends on 00:25 UTC on 3 Oct. (i.e., Oct. 3 @ 2:25 AM CET)** The purpose is to ratify the signalling vote that was taken on Snapshot. The signalling vote was to determine whether or not to even submit it to the Hatch DAO. It passed with 100% voting ‚Äúyes‚Äù. [https://snapshot.org/#/tecommons.eth/proposal/QmRXDFfSQoUzahxjuVGKspXD8NbwoR38CvUSU135vkNZEr](https://snapshot.org/#/tecommons.eth/proposal/QmRXDFfSQoUzahxjuVGKspXD8NbwoR38CvUSU135vkNZEr) Following this very clear signal, this vote has been submitted on-chain here for the official vote. Hatchers vote here!! [https://gateway.pinata.cloud/ipfs/QmPV4NnmJEDA9fmh5VnqAdFCfNwZyY4yZgD5ECxpF5keMm/#/0x4625c2c3e1bc9323cc1a9dc312f3188e8de83f42/0x9b54222e0e3d3a6352ff5184f848919591321159/vote/1/](https://gateway.pinata.cloud/ipfs/QmPV4NnmJEDA9fmh5VnqAdFCfNwZyY4yZgD5ECxpF5keMm/#/0x4625c2c3e1bc9323cc1a9dc312f3188e8de83f42/0x9b54222e0e3d3a6352ff5184f848919591321159/vote/1/)

WOW! Feed the Hungry in Chilliwack BC has raised over 30 ETH on Giveth! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f92f.png" width=20 height=20>

What started as a family effort to make & give sandwiches to the homeless has received overwhelming donor support! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f96a.png" width=20 height=20>

The impact is HUGE: Staying true to their mission to provide resources to the needy, they are expanding to give support to those affected by catastrophic flooding in BC, Canada <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f4a6.png" width=20 height=20>

Check out the full update on their project page:

[https://giveth.io/project/Feed-the-Hungry-in-Chilliwack-BC-Canada](https://giveth.io/project/Feed-the-Hungry-in-Chilliwack-BC-Canada)

GM folks, I'm a community builder at [https://bip.so/](https://bip.so/) Bip.so is a free collaborative workspace for communities. It has a git enabled workflow, deep integrations with Discord, and a social feature to onboard new contributors. Docs can also be translated to multiple languages to enable seamless collaboration. Here's a demo video- [https://youtu.be/QQHMsz2wf2Y](https://youtu.be/QQHMsz2wf2Y) Can someone tell me who I can connect with regarding this? The tool will act as a booster to the community.

Collaborate with the world's best Makers to Co-create products.

**What is ‚ÄúOurVerse and the SolarPunk awakening‚Äù?**

It‚Äôs an immersive video guide that will take the students from learning how to use decentralized coordination tools and techniques to successfully applying them into re-imagining and regenerating their cities.

**What problem is it solving?**

A lack of media showing engaging optimistic visions of the future, and the sectors working in shaping a better future such as web3 and commoning are not reaching the masses because language is too technical, boring, or not relatable. We cannot drive towards a better life if we are not able to imagine it

**How is the problem being solved?**

By teaching through an immersive designed experience. Utilizing compelling narratives, simulation-based learning, and virtual reality to turn lessons into knowledge that our brains are naturally wired to process.

**What is ‚ÄúOurVerse and the SolarPunk awakening‚Äù?**

It‚Äôs an immersive video guide that will take the students from learning how to use decentralized coordination tools and techniques to successfully applying them into re-imagining and regenerating their cities.

**What problem is it solving?**

A lack of media showing engaging optimistic visions of the future, and the sectors working in shaping a better future such as web3 and commoning are not reaching the masses because language is too technical, boring, or not relatable. We cannot drive towards a better life if we are not able to imagine it

**How is the problem being solved?**

By teaching through an immersive designed experience. Utilizing compelling narratives, simulation-based learning, and virtual reality to turn lessons into knowledge that our brains are naturally wired to process.

Hello all <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f642.png" width=20 height=20>

I‚Äôm fundraising for Atuutuu (Trustlines‚Äô chapter in Myanmar) on Gitcoin Grants! Atuutuu is a safe, easy and effective e-voucher system for people caught in humanitarian crises. Our mobile application enables donors and beneficiaries to send and receive e-vouchers that can be exchanged for local goods and services. Local shops can then re-use these e-vouchers to pay suppliers, limiting the need for physical cash and ensuring that economic benefits stay within a community. Atuutuu means ‚Äútogether‚Äù in Burmese, and we‚Äôve combined the best of Universal Basic Income (‚ÄúUBI‚Äù), Unconditional Cash Transfers (‚ÄúUCT‚Äù), and Community Currencies. Every donation counts because of Gitcoin‚Äôs matching plan. If you contribute $1, they will match $22. If you contribute $10, they will match $54

[https://gitcoin.co/grants/5009/change-lives-and-transform-the-system](https://gitcoin.co/grants/5009/change-lives-and-transform-the-system)

Thank you very much! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f604.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f4b0.png" width=20 height=20>

A Hitchhiker's Guide to Token Engineering | Grants

"A Hitchhiker's Guide to Token Engineering‚Äú is a crowdsourced and crowdfunded book and online content repo for token designers, entrepreneurs and applied researchers to get the hang of Token Engineering. The book aims at giving the full account of experience with an end-to-end tool chain: from co-designing the digital ecosystem through games, to...

Hey TEC friends! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f44b.png" width=20 height=20>

Good news from Commons Stack:

**We are officially launching the Commons Prize!** <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f3c6.png" width=20 height=20>

We are looking for the next community to work hand-in-hand with in order to deploy a Commons based on our cultural and technical design patterns. The winning community will work closely with the Commons Stack team to launch their own regenerative token economy, get connected with token economics experts, and benefit from Trusted Seed members as early co-vestors. Find all the details in this Medium article:

[https://medium.com/commonsstack/announcing-the-commons-prize-d3df343c37a9](https://medium.com/commonsstack/announcing-the-commons-prize-d3df343c37a9) <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f4e2.png" width=20 height=20>

_08-Jun-22 02:15 PM_:
Hello my dear friends! Marcus from Cohere (

[https://cohere.network/)](https://cohere.network/))

dropping by here! Gitcoin‚Äôs Grant Round 14 launched today and we‚Äôre so glad to share that Cohere has been accepted in the Climate Solutions category! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f389.png" width=20 height=20>

Gitcoin is the leading web3 crowdfunding platform that supports the democratic funding of public goods. Gitcoin's Climate Solutions funding round (which will take place from June 8th-June 23rd) is all about impact; the kind of impact that Cohere wants to make through on-site regenerative practices and economic/governance structure powered by web3. Gitcoin works like other crowdfunding platforms you might be familiar with (think Kickstarter and Indiegogo), but uses a fund matching mechanism based on community participation. This model places more precedence on the diversity of contributors rather than the amount funded by each contributor; many hands makes light work! Add Gitcoin's matched funding to the mix, and we can see matches up to 20-50x what we raise on our own! Would love to get your support on both our grant, as well all of the other amazing public goods that are currently raising funds on Gitcoin. As far as next steps go: 1. Set up your Gitcoin account on

[https://gitcoin.co/](https://gitcoin.co/)

and verify your identity here:

[https://passport.gitcoin.co/](https://passport.gitcoin.co/)

2. You can donate to our Gitcoin grant here (remember, even just a dollar can go a really long way!):

[https://gitcoin.co/grants/5890/cohere](https://gitcoin.co/grants/5890/cohere)

3. While you‚Äôre on the site, make sure you‚Äôre checking out some of the other amazing grants 4. Share the grant with your community and ask them to support public goods! BONUS: Retweet and like our announcement:

[https://twitter.com/coherenetwork/status/1534589203316621323](https://twitter.com/coherenetwork/status/1534589203316621323)
